<script>
	// Handles the "Show 5 More" button logic for resource filters
(function() {
  function setupShowMore(sectionSelector) {
    var sections = document.querySelectorAll(sectionSelector);
    sections.forEach(function(section) {
      var wrappers = section.querySelectorAll('.filter-wrapper');
      if (wrappers.length <= 5) return;
      var shown = 5;
      // Hide all after the first 5
      wrappers.forEach(function(w, i) {
        if (i >= shown) w.style.display = 'none';
      });
      // Create the button
      var btn = document.createElement('button');
      btn.type = 'button';
      btn.className = 'filter-show-more body-md-500';
      btn.textContent = 'Show 5 More';
  
      section.appendChild(btn);
      btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
        var next = shown + 5;
        for (var i = shown; i < next && i < wrappers.length; i++) {
          wrappers[i].style.display = '';
          wrappers[i].classList.add('is-fading-in');
          // Force reflow for transition
          void wrappers[i].offsetWidth;
          wrappers[i].style.opacity = 0;
          setTimeout((function(wrapper) {
            return function() {
              wrapper.style.opacity = 1;
              wrapper.classList.remove('is-fading-in');
            }
          })(wrappers[i]), 10);
        }
        shown = next;
        if (shown >= wrappers.length) {
          btn.style.display = 'none';
        }
      });
    });
  }
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // Apply "Show 5 More" only to filter sections that are NOT the Type section
    // Temporarily disabled - uncomment to restore "Show 5 More" functionality
    // setupShowMore('.resource-filters .filter-section:not(#type-filter-section)');
  });
})();

</script>

					<div class="search-sort-container">

	<script>
		// Collapsible footer toggle
		$(document).ready(function() {
			$('.collapsible-footer-toggle').on('click', function() {
				$('.collapsible-footer-content').slideToggle();
				$(this).toggleClass('active');
				if (!$(this).hasClass('active')) {
					$(this).addClass('inactive-animate');
				} else {
					$(this).removeClass('inactive-animate');
				}
				$(this).find('.inactive, .active').toggle();
			});

else{card.style.display='none';}});if(showMoreBtn){if(visibleCount>=cards.length){showMoreBtn.style.display='none';}else{showMoreBtn.style.display='block';}}};this.initShowMoreResourceCards=function(){updateShowMoreButton();if(showMoreBtn){showMoreBtn.addEventListener('click',function(){const searchTerm=searchInput.value.toLowerCase();const activeFilters=document.querySelectorAll('.resource-filters input:checked');let filterObj={'topics':[],'type':[],'product':[]};for(let index=0;index<activeFilters.length;index++){const element=activeFilters[index];filterObj[element.className].push(element.name);}
const checkedSortCheckbox=document.querySelector('.search-sort-container .select__options input[type="checkbox"]:checked');const sortVal=checkedSortCheckbox?checkedSortCheckbox.value:'latest';const webinarsSelected=filterObj.type.includes('webinars');const filteredPosts=allPosts.filter(post=>{if(searchTerm){const titleMatch=post.title.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm);const excerptMatch=post.excerpt.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm);if(!titleMatch&&!excerptMatch)return false;}
if(filterObj.type.length>0){let primaryType='';if(post.type){if(Array.isArray(post.type)&&post.type.length>0){primaryType=post.type[0].slug||post.type[0];}else if(typeof post.type==='string'){primaryType=post.type.split(/,\s*/)[0];}}
if(primaryType==='upcomingwebinars'&&webinarsSelected){return true;}
const hasMatchingType=filterObj.type.includes(primaryType);if(!hasMatchingType)return false;}
if(filterObj.topics.length>0){let postTopics=[];if(post.topic){if(Array.isArray(post.topic)){postTopics=post.topic.map(t=>t.slug||t);}else if(typeof post.topic==='string'){postTopics=post.topic.split(/,\s*/);}}
const hasMatchingTopic=filterObj.topics.some(filterTopic=>postTopics.some(postTopic=>postTopic===filterTopic));if(!hasMatchingTopic)return false;}
if(filterObj.product.length>0){let postProducts=[];if(post.products){if(Array.isArray(post.products)){postProducts=post.products.map(p=>p.slug||p);}else if(typeof post.products==='string'){postProducts=post.products.split(/,\s*/);}}
const hasMatchingProduct=filterObj.product.some(filterProduct=>postProducts.some(postProduct=>postProduct===filterProduct));if(!hasMatchingProduct)return false;}
return true;});let sortedPosts=[...filteredPosts];if(webinarsSelected){let upcomingWebinars=sortedPosts.filter(post=>isPostOfType(post,'upcomingwebinars'));const otherPosts=sortedPosts.filter(post=>!isPostOfType(post,'upcomingwebinars'));upcomingWebinars=upcomingWebinars.filter(post=>matchesFilters(post,filterObj,searchTerm));if(sortVal==='az'){upcomingWebinars.sort((a,b)=>a.title.localeCompare(b.title));otherPosts.sort((a,b)=>a.title.localeCompare(b.title));}else if(sortVal==='za'){upcomingWebinars.sort((a,b)=>b.title.localeCompare(a.title));otherPosts.sort((a,b)=>b.title.localeCompare(a.title));}else if(sortVal==='oldest'){upcomingWebinars.reverse();otherPosts.reverse();}
sortedPosts=[...upcomingWebinars,...otherPosts];}else{if(sortVal==='az'){sortedPosts.sort((a,b)=>a.title.localeCompare(b.title));}else if(sortVal==='za'){sortedPosts.sort((a,b)=>b.title.localeCompare(a.title));}else if(sortVal==='oldest'){sortedPosts.reverse();}}
visibleCount+=CARDS_PER_PAGE;const toRender=sortedPosts.slice(0,visibleCount);let postsHTML='';if(toRender.length>0){toRender.forEach(post=>{postsHTML+=createCardHTML(post);});}
postsContainer.innerHTML=postsHTML;if(visibleCount>=sortedPosts.length){showMoreBtn.style.display='none';}else{showMoreBtn.style.display='block';}});}};this.initCustomSortDropdown=function(){const root=document.querySelector('.select');if(!root)return;const trigger=root.querySelector('.select__trigger');const label=trigger.querySelector('.select__label');const options=root.querySelector('.select__options');const checkboxes=options.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');trigger.addEventListener('click',function(e){const isOpen=root.getAttribute('data-state')==='open';root.setAttribute('data-state',isOpen?'':'open');trigger.setAttribute('aria-expanded',!isOpen);if(!isOpen){setTimeout(()=>{const checked=options.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]:checked');if(checked)checked.focus();},0);}});checkboxes.forEach(checkbox=>{checkbox.addEventListener('change',function(e){if(this.checked){checkboxes.forEach(cb=>{if(cb!==this)cb.checked=false;});label.textContent=this.parentElement.textContent.trim();setTimeout(()=>filterAndRenderPosts(),50);}else{this.checked=true;}});});let checked=Array.from(checkboxes).filter(cb=>cb.checked);if(checked.length===0){checkboxes[0].checked=true;label.textContent=checkboxes[0].parentElement.textContent.trim();}else{label.textContent=checked[0].parentElement.textContent.trim();}
document.addEventListener('mousedown',function(e){if(!root.contains(e.target)){root.setAttribute('data-state','');trigger.setAttribute('aria-expanded',false);}});};}
return new Constructor();}());ResourceCenterEvents=(function(){function Constructor(){function dlPush(obj){(window.dataLayer=window.dataLayer||[]).push(obj);}
const searchInput=document.getElementById('resource-search');const sidebarFilters=document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar input[type="checkbox"]');const sortCheckboxes=document.querySelectorAll('.sort-checkbox input[type="checkbox"]');this.init=function(){this.initSearchTracking();this.initFilterTracking();this.initSortTracking();};this.initSearchTracking=function(){let t;searchInput?.addEventListener('input',e=>{clearTimeout(t);t=setTimeout(()=>{const term=e.target.value.trim();const eventObject={event:'resource_search_text',resource_search_term:term};console.log('Resource search used:',eventObject);if(term)dlPush(eventObject);},300);});};this.initFilterTracking=function(){sidebarFilters.forEach(el=>el.addEventListener('change',e=>{if(!e.target.checked)return;const checkboxType=e.target.classList.contains('topics')?'topic':e.target.classList.contains('type')?'type':e.target.classList.contains('product')?'product':'unknown';const eventObject={event:'resource_filter',resource_checkbox_type:checkboxType,resource_checkbox_value:e.target.name,resource_filter_id:e.target.id};console.log('Resource filter used:',eventObject);dlPush(eventObject);}));};this.initSortTracking=function(){sortCheckboxes.forEach(el=>el.addEventListener('change',e=>{if(!e.target.checked)return;const eventObject={event:'resource_sort',resource_sort_option:e.target.value};console.log('Resource sort used:',eventObject);dlPush(eventObject);}));};}
return new Constructor();}());</script>
